;----------------------------------------------------------------------------
;AI helper
;----------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Statedef 10000]
ctrl=0

[State 10000,間違いで本体が来たら立ちへ移行]
type=selfstate
trigger1=!ishelper
value=0

[State 10000]
type=varset
trigger1=!var(1) || !(root,alive) || roundstate!=2 || root,var(57)
var(0)=1

[State 10000,ﾌﾗｸﾞON]
type=parentvarset
triggerall=!var(0)
trigger1=(root,command="up")||(root,command="down")||(root,command="back")||(root,command="fwd")||(root,command="a")||(root,command="b")||(root,command="c")||(root,command="x")||(root,command="y")
trigger2=(root,command="z")||(root,command="s")||(root,command="fbdf_4")||(root,command="spspsp")||(root,command="fbdf_44")||(root,command="dbdb_2")||(root,command="dbdb_1")||(root,command="dbdb_3")||(root,command="dbdb_9")
trigger3=(root,command="df_1117")||(root,command="df_118")||(root,command="gura")||(root,command="df_1")||(root,command="df_2")||(root,command="df_3")||(root,command="df_4")||(root,command="db_1")||(root,command="db_2")
trigger4=(root,command="db_3")||(root,command="db_4")||(root,command="df_111")||(root,command="df_1112")||(root,command="df_1114")||(root,command="feni")||(root,command="sword")||(root,command="FF")||(root,command="BB")||(root,command="call")
trigger5=(root,command="scall")||(root,command="recovery")||(root,command="dodge")||(root,command="down_x")||(root,command="down_y")||(root,command="down_z")||(root,command="fwd_a")||(root,command="fwd_b")||(root,command="fwd_c")||(root,command="fwd_x")
trigger6=(root,command="fwd_y")||(root,command="fd_y")||(root,command="fwd_z")||(root,command="back_a")||(root,command="back_b")||(root,command="back_c")||(root,command="back_x")||(root,command="back_y")||(root,command="back_z")||(root,command="fd_b")
trigger7=(root,command="fd_a")||(root,command="down_a")||(root,command="down_b")||(root,command="down_c")||(root,command="longjump")||(root,command="sp1")||(root,command="sp2")
var(57)=-2

[State 10000]
type=parentvarset
triggerall= !var(0)&&(root,var(57)=-2)
Trigger1=(command="a"&&root,command="a")||(command="b"&&root,command="b")||(command="c"&&root,command="c")||(command="x"&&root,command="x")||(command="y"&&root,command="y")||(command="z"&&root,command="z")||(command="s"&&root,command="s")
trigger2=(command="up"&&root,command="up")||(command="down"&&root,command="down")||(command="back"&&root,command="back")||(command="fwd"&&root,command="fwd")
var(57) = -1

[State 10000]
type=varset
triggerall= var(0)
trigger1= var(0)=1
trigger1= var(0):=0
trigger2= root,command="fwd" || root,command="back" || root,command="up" || root,command="down"
trigger3= root,command="a" || root,command="b" || root,command="c"
trigger4= root,command="x" || root,command="y" || root,command="z"
trigger5= root,command="s"
var(0)=1

[State 10000,立ったら消失]
type=destroyself
triggerall= var(1):=1
trigger1= root,var(57)
trigger2= !(root,alive)
trigger3= roundstate!=2



;---------------------------------------------------------------------------
[Statedef -1]
;---------------------------------------------------------------------------
[State -1, AI起動用ヘルパー]
type=helper
trigger1=!NumHelper(10000+ID)&&!IsHelper&&roundstate=2&&alive&&!var(57)
helpertype=normal
name="AI"
stateno=10000
ID=10000+ID
pos=9999,9999
keyctrl=1
pausemovetime=2147483647
supermovetime=2147483647
persistent = 0

[State -1, ↑が余計なことしないように]
type=changestate
trigger1= ishelper(10000+ID)
trigger1= stateno!=10000
value=10000

[State -1, AIflagset]
type = VarSet
triggerall = RoundState = 2 && !IsHelper && var(57) = [-2,0]
trigger1 = var(57)=-2
Trigger2 = (Command = "a" ^^ Command = "a2") || (Command = "b" ^^ Command = "b2") || (Command = "c" ^^ Command = "c2") || (Command = "x" ^^ Command = "x2") || (Command = "y" ^^ Command = "y2") || (Command = "z" ^^ Command = "z2")
trigger3 = (Command = "s" ^^ Command = "s2") || (Command = "holdfwd" ^^ Command = "holdfwd2") || (Command = "holdback" ^^ Command = "holdback2") || (Command = "holdup" ^^ Command = "holdup2") || (Command = "holddown" ^^ Command = "holddown2")
Trigger4 = Command="AI1"||Command="AI2"||Command="AI3"||Command="AI4"||Command="AI5"||Command="AI6"||Command="AI7"||Command="AI8"||Command="AI9"||Command="AI10"||Command="AI11"||Command="AI12"||Command="AI13"||Command="AI14"||Command="AI15"
Trigger5 = Command="AI16"||Command="AI17"||Command="AI18"||Command="AI19"||Command="AI20"||Command="AI21"||Command="AI22"||Command="AI23"||Command="AI24"||Command="AI25"||Command="AI26"||Command="AI27"||Command="AI28"||Command="AI29"
Trigger6 = Command="AI30"||Command="AI31"||Command="AI32"||Command="AI33"||Command="AI34"
ignorehitpause = 1

var(57) = 10	;0,1-2,3-5,6-7,8-10,11  ←AIレベル設定  11は超反応あり

;ためし
;------------------------------------------------------------------------

[State 701, 2];ボタン連打で終了させる
type = varadd
triggerall = var(28) >= -5
trigger1 = var(28) <= 5
trigger1 = var(57) > 5
var(28) = -1

;------------------------------------------------------------------------

;---------------------------------------------------------------------------
; AI_halper
;---------------------------------------------------------------------------

[State -1, ]
type = Helper
trigger1 = !NumHelper(92) && (var(57) > 7) && !IsHelper
ID = 92
name = "AIhelper1"
pos = 130,9999
postype = p1
stateno = 92
persistent = 0
keyctrl = 0
ownpal = 1
Ignorehitpause = 1

[State -1, ]
type = Helper
trigger1 = !NumHelper(93) && (var(57) > 7) && !IsHelper
ID = 93
facing = -1
name = "AIhelper2"
pos = -100,9999
postype = p1
stateno = 93
persistent = 0
keyctrl = 0
ownpal = 1
Ignorehitpause = 1


;反応速度
;------------------------------------------------------------------------
[State -1, 0]
type = VarSet
triggerall = GameTime % 100 = 0
trigger1 = (var(2)/100) > 0
var(2) = var(2) - (var(2)/100)*100

[State -1, 0]
type = VarSet
triggerall = GameTime % 100 = 0
triggerall = (var(2)/100) = 0
trigger1 = var(59) = [6,10]
var(2) = var(2) + ((90 - (var(59)-6)*15) - (random%(61 - (var(59)-6)*9)))*100

[State -1, 0]
type = VarSet
triggerall = GameTime % 100 = 0
triggerall = var(59) = [6,10]
trigger1 = var(59) = 6
trigger1 = random%100 = [0,1]
trigger2 = var(59) = [7,10]
trigger2 = random%100 = [0,((var(59)-6)*5 - 1)]
trigger3 = var(59) >= 11
var(2) = var(2) - (var(2)/100)*100

[State -1, 0]
type = VarSet
trigger1 = P2MoveType = A && ((var(2)%100) < 99)
var(2) = var(2) + 1

[State -1, 0]
type = VarSet
trigger1 = P2MoveType != A && ((var(2)%100) > 0)
var(2) = var(2) - var(2)%100


;ストライカー呼び出し可能変数
;-------------------------------------------------------------------------
[State -1, ]
type = VarSet
triggerall = !IsHelper
triggerall = var(3)%10 = 0
triggerall = var(27) = 0
trigger1 = movetype != H      ;食らい時以外で
trigger1 = stateno != 0       ;ニュ?トラル状態からは不可?！
trigger1 = stateno != 11      ;
trigger1 = stateno != 20      ;
trigger1 = stateno != 21      ;
